4139 /*
4140 * This function searches the compressed table efficiently.
4141 */
4142 static unsigned long
4143 ft_get_adobe_glyph_index( const char* name,
4144 const char* limit )
4145 {
4146 int c = 0;
4147 int count, min, max;
4148 const unsigned char* p = ft_adobe_glyph_list;
4149
4150
4151 if ( name == 0 || name >= limit )
4152 goto NotFound;
4153
4154 c = *name++;
4155 count = p[1];
4156 p += 2;
4157
4158 min = 0;
4159 max = count;
4160
4161 while ( min < max )
4162 {
4163 int mid = ( min + max ) >> 1;
4164 const unsigned char* q = p + mid * 2;
4165 int c2;
4166
4167
4168 q = ft_adobe_glyph_list + ( ( (int)q[0] << 8 ) | q[1] );
4169
4170 c2 = q[0] & 127;
4171 if ( c2 == c )
4172 {
4173 p = q;
4174 goto Found;
4175 }
4176 if ( c2 < c )
4177 min = mid + 1;
4178 else
4179 max = mid;
4180 }
4181 goto NotFound;
4182
4183 Found:
4184 for (;;)
4185 {
4186 /* assert (*p & 127) == c */
4187
4188 if ( name >= limit )
4189 {
4190 if ( (p[0] & 128) == 0 &&
4191 (p[1] & 128) != 0 )
4192 return (unsigned long)( ( (int)p[2] << 8 ) | p[3] );
4193
4194 goto NotFound;
4195 }
4196 c = *name++;
4197 if ( p[0] & 128 )
4198 {
4199 p++;
4200 if ( c != (p[0] & 127) )
4201 goto NotFound;
4202
4203 continue;
4204 }
4205
4206 p++;
4207 count = p[0] & 127;
4208 if ( p[0] & 128 )
4209 p += 2;
4210
4211 p++;
4212
4213 for ( ; count > 0; count--, p += 2 )
4214 {
4215 int offset = ( (int)p[0] << 8 ) | p[1];
4216 const unsigned char* q = ft_adobe_glyph_list + offset;
4217
4218 if ( c == ( q[0] & 127 ) )
4219 {
4220 p = q;
4221 goto NextIter;
4222 }
4223 }
4224 goto NotFound;
4225
4226 NextIter:
4227 ;
4228 }
4229
4230 NotFound:
4231 return 0;
4232 }
